  <script>
   var bdc = bdc || {};
	bdc.adLayers = bdc.adLayers || {};
	bdc.adLayers.getCurrentBreakPoint = function() {
		if ( window.outerWidth < 768 ) { return 'mobile'; }
		if ( window.outerWidth < 960 ) { return 'tablet'; }
		return 'desktop';
	};
	bdc.adLayers.getTestQueryString = function() {
		var queryString = window.location.search;
		var regex = /[\?\&]test=([^&]*)/;
		return queryString.match( regex ) ? queryString.match( regex )[1] : '';
	};
	bdc.adLayers.getRefQueryString = function() {
		var queryString = window.location.search;
		var regex = /[\?\&]ref=([^&]*)/;
		return queryString.match( regex ) ? queryString.match( regex )[1] : '';
	};
	bdc.adLayers.ilPresent = function() {
		// Check for presence of instart logic.
		return 'undefined' !== typeof( window._bcm_il ) ? 'true' : 'false';
	};
  </script>
